                  <hi rend="ital">I went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">turned, from him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, to another:</hi> whence, it is said, the saying in the Kur [xlii. 35], <foreign lang="ar">وَمَنْ يَعْشُ عَنْ ذِكْرِ ٱلرَّحْمٰنِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And such as turns from the admonition of the Compassionate</hi>]. (S. See another explanation of this saying in what follows.)
